<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a> (2647)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1_3">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">slange</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">slango</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*slangô</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:snake.html>snake</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:serpent.html>serpent</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_8"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slangen.html>slangen</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slangetje.html>slangetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:snake.html>snake</a>, squamate <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> suborder Serpentes

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_3">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></i>.

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:older.html>older</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:slede.html>slede</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">slēde</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*slido</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*slidô</i>.
</p>

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*slaihwō</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(<a href = vnd.unilang:s.html>s</a>)leie-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bluish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <a href = vnd.unilang:related.html>related</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">slåen</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:perhaps.html>perhaps</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">сли́ва</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slíva</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:plum.html>plum</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:slijten.html>slijten</a> (13440)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sliten</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*slītan</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*slītaną</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:slims.html>slims</a> (31581)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:low.html>Low</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml"><a href = vnd.unilang:slim.html>slim</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:slim.html>slim</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:twisted.html>twisted</a>, crooked; <a href = vnd.unilang:bad.html>bad</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:evil.html>evil</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <a href = vnd.unilang:compare.html>compare</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:also.html>also</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">schlimm</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:bad.html>bad</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:evil.html>evil</a>; (<a href = vnd.unilang:col.html>col</a>.) <a href = vnd.unilang:sick.html>sick</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <a href = vnd.unilang:first.html>First</a> attested <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> 17th <a href = vnd.unilang:century.html>century</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:mostly.html>mostly</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> meanings <a href = vnd.unilang:such.html>such</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:as.html>as</a> “bad”, “useless”, “inappropriate”, “evil”, <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> “wild”, <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:more.html>more</a> rarely “sick”. <a href = vnd.unilang:this.html>This</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:last.html>last</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meaning.html>meaning</a> “sick” <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:apparently.html>apparently</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:more.html>more</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:frequent.html>frequent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:southern.html>Southern</a> Kurzeme dialects; <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> Vidzeme, <a href = vnd.unilang:this.html>this</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meaning.html>meaning</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:not.html>not</a> attested <a href = vnd.unilang:still.html>still</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> 18th <a href = vnd.unilang:century.html>century</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:it.html>It</a> became <a href = vnd.unilang:more.html>more</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:frequent.html>frequent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:written.html>written</a> Latvian <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:works.html>works</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gotthard_Friedrich_Stender" class="extiw" title="w:Gotthard Friedrich Stender"><a href = vnd.unilang:g.html>G</a>. F. Stenders</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:late.html>late</a> 18th <a href = vnd.unilang:century.html>century</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:especially.html>especially</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:his.html>his</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dictionary.html>dictionary</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:which.html>which</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:krank.html>krank</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:translated.html>translated</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:as.html>as</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv"><a href = vnd.unilang:slims.html>slims</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:which.html>which</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv"><a href = vnd.unilang:slims.html>slims</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:no.html>no</a> longer <a href = vnd.unilang:translated.html>translated</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:as.html>as</a> “bad,” “useless”. Stenders <a href = vnd.unilang:also.html>also</a> coined <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">slimība</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">slimnieks</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">apslimt</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">slimēties</i> (<a href = vnd.unilang:but.html>but</a> curiously <a href = vnd.unilang:not.html>not</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">slimot</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:which.html>which</a> appeared <a href = vnd.unilang:only.html>only</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> 19th <a href = vnd.unilang:century.html>century</a>).<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
